CREATE TABLE airlines (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, website STRING);

CREATE TABLE bookings (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, flight_id UUID REFERENCES flights(id), passenger_name STRING, passenger_email STRING, booking_date TIMESTAMP);</t><s>UPDATE flights SET departure_time = '10:00:00' WHERE destination_id = '123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000';</s>

CREATE TABLE flights (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, destination_id UUID REFERENCES destinations(id), flight_number STRING, departure_date TIMESTAMP, departure_time TIME, arrival_date TIMESTAMP, arrival_time TIME);</t><s>UPDATE flights SET departure_time = '10:00:00' WHERE destination_id = '123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000';</s>

CREATE TABLE flights (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, destination_id UUID REFERENCES destinations(id), flight_number STRING, departure_date TIMESTAMP, departure_time TIME, arrival_date TIMESTAMP, arrival_time TIME);

CREATE TABLE airlines (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, website STRING);

CREATE TABLE bookings (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, flight_id UUID REFERENCES flights(id), passenger_name STRING, passenger_email STRING, booking_date TIMESTAMP);</t><s>update bookings set booking_date = '2022-08-20 15:00:00' where id = '123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000';</s>

CREATE TABLE bookings (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, flight_id UUID REFERENCES flights(id), passenger_name STRING, passenger_email STRING, booking_date TIMESTAMP);

CREATE TABLE destinations (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, description STRING);

CREATE TABLE airlines (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, website STRING);</t><s>UPDATE bookings SET booking_date = '2022-08-20 15:00:00' WHERE id = '123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000';</s>
